We are a young family, who have been living here for about 1 year. It's clean, quiet, and I feel safe to walk around with our dog (day or night). One thing makes me disappoint is some residents (NOT ALL) don't like us even though we are cool to everybody. We said "Hi" to them, but they gave us back a cold face :[ (because we are Asian? 2 of my kids have  just started to play softball for the first time this year. This is where it all comes together them and their teammates. Mostly they use the complex for practices. There have been a few games as well.  There are 4 baseball fields and although it seems like a fairly small place , it seems to fit perfectly in with its location setting. I think the people behind the works of it all are the ones who make this all happen for their community.
They have restrooms & Yes there is a snack bar as well. Its open during game time and they have just as many snacks too eat as the other fields we play at. Every time we come here it has proven to be a safe, clean and a fun place for kids to come together and play and is used for its very purpose. Occasionally we are a little confused on who's playing where, but maybe that's a good sign of more kids playing and maybe even a bigger complex one day. Batters up!<//Text>

<UserId.>110095308517014473199< /UserId.>< name>
Debbie Minter< /name>
< Time>
1620849382949<//Time>
<Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
This bookstore is amazing!  They have a wonderful supply of books about feminism, race, and social justice issues, fiction as well as nonfiction. There also have a kids and young adults section.  They sell items supporting black-owned businesses - snacks, Oak Park gifts and t-shirts, journals, etc.  They have a cozy sitting area and friendly, helpful customer service.  One drawback is the #of books stocked (probably due to space limitations) but they will gladly order any book for you.  Occasionally book orders take awhile but the staff is very communicative about delays - just don't order from here if you're in a hurry without checking on the delivery date first.< /Text>

< Review>
This was my first time coming to underground books. This was for a private event . The bookstore is wonderful with a amazing variety/selection of books along with comfortable seating. It is neat and well organized and had plenty of holiday decor and books on display for the season. I will definitely be back to peruse the shelves since I love reading. If you are a person who likes/loves to read and like being able to  turn a  page or use a bookmark you'll enjoy this bookstore.< /Review>

What a lovely shopping experience my 2 friends and I had yesterday at the Underground Bookshop!  The ambiance of the shop draws you in and the two young women clerks were so helpful and fun. I have been buying from this dispensary for the past couple of months and I can say it's one of the best dispensaries that I've bought from. The drivers are friendly, the product is great, and everything is delivered in a timely fashion. The only complaint I have about them is their lack of communication about their point system. A few weeks ago, I had asked one of their drivers about how to redeem my points and I was told that they were still trying to figure out how it was all going to work. I also called and had a rude interaction with one of their employees. I asked him how I could redeem my points that I had accumulated since October because it wasn't showing up on my account. He told me that they had switched over to a company that wouldn't honor the points that were previously earned before they had switched. I voiced my opinion on how I thought it was unfair because it seemed like false advertising to me. I told him that their point system is what led me to buy from them. His response was, "Well realistically, you bought the weed because you wanted the weed." Yes, I obviously bought the weed because I wanted it, but I stopped giving my business to other dispensaries. I had spent $1000 and was looking forward to redeeming $200 off my order only to be told that my previous points weren't going to be counted. If you didn't know how the point system was going to work, I don't think it should have been advertised. It's a bit frustrating that this is how I was treated.

This is the only bad interaction I've had with them. They've always been friendly and their delivery services are very convenient. This one bad experience isn't going to stop me from buying from them, but I would just like to be treated kindly next time.< /review>

We know the ‚Äúone hour delivery‚Äù isn‚Äôt guaranteed, but if we‚Äôre putting in an order a couple hours ahead of the delivery time we prefer, we don‚Äôt understand why it‚Äôs always late. We‚Äôve had mishaps with our orders not even being sent out. We never leave reviews about anything, and for Kingdom, we‚Äôve been a little torn on whether we should, a driver recommended that we voice our concerns in a review, so here we are. Don‚Äôt get us wrong, the price is great, especially for it being local. Local, is a huge plus and the quality is usually amazing, even better than Cookies, in our opinion. We‚Äôre sure they‚Äôre busy, but there has to be a way to manage things a little better. And we‚Äôre still waiting to hear what they‚Äôre suppose to be doing with the point system. All in all, the price is great, local is a huge plus, and the product is top shelf quality, but they do have some kinks to work out and we understand that.

< Review>
I consider myself a connoisseur of fine Mexican cuisine ever since I traveled the Yucatan peninsula in '74. I've been there and back 9 times since, and never had I encountered Frijoles (beans) as genuinely Mexican as these at La Placita. You can taste the Mexican soil in which these beans were grown. I just happened upon this hidden treasure nearly 20 years ago when I was in Florin Town picking up some Caterpillar parts at Florin Tractor, they recommended Placita as I was in search of a good Menudo spot. My taste buds have never experienced anything like their Frijoles and Enchiladas North of the Rio Grand! Exquisite< /Review>

<user_name>Joseph Kohler< /user_name><date>1546540912703</date>< review>
Glad to see the food was fresh even with the holiday schedule.  Last day off of holiday vacation and my usual place was not open.  Picked Bamboo as a last ditch option to get something different than the holiday chow I was getting over the last 10 days.   All aspects that I saw were clean and tidy.  We sat at the bar so saw the chef work.  No complaints and nothing to worry about in regards to his methods.  Got a few different rolls and each was distinctly different.  Considering the components are limited with sushi, they found good combinations.  Also, some ingredients were not standard which was refreshing.  Service was friendly, food was tasty and the atmosphere was comfortable.  I would try again to see if this place becomes our new standard sushi joint.  Prices are a bit higher than some other places but I got good quality which is necessary for sushi.< /review>

Excellent quality and creative presentation.  Many dishes are presented with artistic flare as shown in my pictures. Staff is attentive and the decor has a modern feel to it.   Toro is good and priced well.  Uni is limited and usually available only on weekends.  There are a few signature dishes on the menu that are worth making the trip to check out if you live in the south bay.</review>

I was recently in need of a small storage unit and found the rates here to be perfect. They were the cheapest in the valley. I went to take a tour and see if I liked it or not but was worried as I was cutting it close to their closing time.
